He finds this trend noteworthy, given the macroeconomic factors at play. Despite the rising U.S. dollar and 10-year Treasury Yields, along with a decreasing global M2 money supply, Coutts believes that Bitcoin can serve as a diversifier of risk and enhance risk-adjusted returns. He cited improvements in Bitcoin's risk-adjusted returns, measured using the #Sortino ratio, during the last two bear markets.\n\nRecognizing Bitcoin's relatively short history, Coutts stated that holding the cryptocurrency through multiple economic cycles has proven advantageous.
